9th - 32nd Decklists
====================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX KUALA LUMPUR 2016](/en/events/coverage/gpkl16)
 on October 23, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim












 With Pro Tour *Kaladesh* recently concluding and the metagame taking a turn, you must be curious what performed well at Grand Prix Kuala Lumpur. Here are the top performing decks and do keep in mind that a few of these inventors were only a win or two away from the Top 8!

##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
